</td>

<tr>
<td rowspan="1" colspan="1">
<p><strong>27</strong>
</p>
</td>
<td rowspan="1" colspan="1">
<p><strong>GST Voucher Portal</strong>
</p>
</td>
<td rowspan="1" colspan="1">
<p>The GST Voucher was introduced by the Government in Budget 2012 to help
lower-income Singaporeans. The GST Voucher is given in three components-
Cash, Medisave and U-Save. The website provides general information of
the GST Voucher scheme and allows citizens to perform online transactions
such as checking their eligibility for the scheme.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td rowspan="1" colspan="1">
<p><strong>28</strong>
</p>
</td>
<td rowspan="1" colspan="1">
<p><strong>Workfare Portal</strong>
</p>
</td>
<td rowspan="1" colspan="1">
<p>Workfare Portal is a one-stop portal that houses generic information on
the various Workfare schemes. It enables citizens to enquire on their Workfare
eligibility and payment details, access customised advice on actions, access
the Workfare Income Supplement (WIS) calculator, and submit enquiries and
requests to change their payment/ notification mode.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td rowspan="1" colspan="1">
<p><strong>29</strong>
</p>
</td>
<td rowspan="1" colspan="1">
<p><strong>SG Bonus</strong>
</p>
</td>
<td rowspan="1" colspan="1">
<p>The SG Bonus was announced in Budget 2018 to share the fruits of Singapore’s
development with Singaporeans.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td rowspan="1" colspan="1">
<p><strong>30</strong>
</p>
</td>
<td rowspan="1" colspan="1">
<p><strong>Silver Support Scheme</strong>
</p>
</td>
<td rowspan="1" colspan="1">
<p>The Silver Support Scheme website is an online portal for the public to
access generic information on the Silver Support Scheme. Elderly Singaporeans
aged 65 and above may enquire on their Silver Support eligibility, payment
details, and submit enquiries and requests to change their payment mode.</p>
</td>
</tr>

<tr>
<td rowspan="1" colspan="1">
<p><strong>36</strong>
</p>
</td>
<td rowspan="1" colspan="1">
<p><strong>Family Justice Court (FJC)</strong>
</p>
</td>
<td rowspan="1" colspan="1">
<p><strong>iFAMS</strong>
</p>
</td>
<td rowspan="1" colspan="1">
<p>The Integrated Family Application Management System (iFAMS) is a comprehensive
end-to-end system which deals predominantly with applications for family
protection and maintenance order cases brought before the Family Justice
Courts (FJC). It is a paperless system and developed as a base for family
related applications which can cater for future expansion to include other
family court related applications. iFAMS covers electronic case filing,
tracking, workflow routing, case hearing and generation of electronic letters,
Court Orders and statistical reports.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td rowspan="1" colspan="1">
<p><strong>37</strong>
</p>
</td>
<td rowspan="11" colspan="1">
<p><strong>Government Technology Agency (GovTech)</strong>
</p>
</td>
<td rowspan="1" colspan="1">
<p><strong>Covid Support Grant</strong>
</p>
</td>
<td rowspan="1" colspan="1">
<p>One stop portal for applicant for MSF Covid Support Grant</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td rowspan="1" colspan="1">
<p><strong>38</strong>
</p>
</td>
<td rowspan="1" colspan="1">
<p><strong>FormSG</strong>
</p>
</td>
<td rowspan="1" colspan="1">
<p>FormSG is a form builder tool for government agencies to self-serve and
create online forms, with the goal of replacing paper forms. Till date,
it has replaced over 700 paper forms and are used by over 55 agencies such
as MOM, MOE, PA and SportSG.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td rowspan="1" colspan="1">

<p><strong>LifeSG</strong>
</p>
</td>
<td rowspan="1" colspan="1">
<p>LifeSG (formerly Moments of Life) is a mobile app that provides a suite
of services to support citizens’ needs at key junctures. It does so by
integrating and bundling services across different government agencies.&nbsp;</p>
</td>
